                          (seq
                            p7
                            (while
                              (or
                                (and b36 b62 b67 b27) (and
                                                        (or b22 b16 b83) b63
                                                        b84))
                              p7))
                          (test 1)))))))
              (test 1))))))))

(equiv 1)
